Women's National Goods Annual Meeting Preparations Concluded Yesterday

Dispatching Personnel to Liaise with the Student National Goods Annual Meeting

The Women's National Goods Year Movement Committee convened a joint meeting of the Design, Economics, and Work Committees for the ninth time yesterday at 4:00 PM at 80 Hualong Road. Preparations have concluded. Over twenty people attended, including Lin Kecong, Fei Xia, Huang Bingpei, Li Manyun, Sun Daosheng, Xu Jianruo, Wang Hanqiang, Cheng Shouzhong (represented by Zhang Baling), Shen Jinghui, Hu Xiyuan, Pan Yangyao (represented by Sun Daosheng), Tang Guanyu (represented by Huang Bingpei), Ni Baiyan (represented by Wei Taishun), and Li Kangnian (represented by Shen Jinghui). Chairman Lin Kecong reported on the Autumn Clothing Guessing Contest, the National Goods Mobile Exhibition, the Lantern Parade, the Trademark Sample Exhibition, the National Goods Promotion Delegation to other provinces, the inspection of Central and Southern China, and the general financial situation. Discussions then commenced on: (1) Whether the association should hold a closing ceremony at the end of the year to commemorate the conclusion of the Women's National Goods Year Movement. It was resolved that next year will be the Student National Goods Year, and the association can liaise with them for a handover. Personnel will be dispatched to make contact. (2) The association's National Goods Mobile Exhibition has a provision to issue commemorative certificates to participating manufacturers. Please draft a certificate design for printing. It was resolved that the association will draft a design for printing, and all participating manufacturers and contributors will be given certificates. (3) The association's funds are insufficient to cover expenses. Please discuss a solution. It was resolved that the remaining funds from the Shanghai West National Exhibition will be incorporated into the regular allocation for expenses. If there are surplus funds, enamel slogan signs will be widely produced and nailed to utility poles on various streets to arouse public interest in using national goods. (4) Should the staff of the secretariat continue to work after the end of this year? It was resolved that Sun Daosheng should contact the Student National Goods Year Association.

Researchers at the Zhenru Forensic Institute

First Graduation Ceremony

For the First Time in Our Country, Scientific Forensic Doctors

The Ministry of Judicial Administration Issues Forensic Doctor Certificates

To be Assigned to Serve in Provincial High Courts

The first cohort of researchers at the Zhenru Forensic Institute has completed their studies. Having passed the examinations, the Ministry of Judicial Administration has approved the issuance of forensic doctor certificates to Chen Anliang, Zhang Jizhong, Wang Jizu, Chen Kangyi, Li Xinmin, Zhang Shuhuai, Chen Wei, Lü Ruiquan, Yu Xiluan, Cai Bingnan, Chen Rengji, Cai Jiaohui, Bao Xiaowei, Hu Shiyuan, Xie Zhichang, Zhang Chengbiao, Wang Sijian, and others, totaling seventeen individuals. The graduation ceremony was held yesterday morning in the institute's auditorium, with a large number of attendees. Institute Director Dr. Lin Ji announced the significance of the meeting and delivered a speech. Various guests and researchers also gave speeches, making it a grand occasion. It is reported that the graduating researchers were originally medical doctors from various universities in the country and some had served in courts or in the medical field. Their performance was excellent. They will be assigned by the Ministry of Judicial Administration to serve in provincial high courts or introduced to political and police departments to improve forensic medical services. From now on, forensic medical examinations in our country's courts will advance towards a brighter future.

This Year's Cotton Production Greatly Increased

Chinese and Japanese Textile Mills Using Over 500,000 Bales

According to reliable statistics, this year's cotton production in our country has reached over 1.1 million bales, an increase of over 10% compared to last year. As a result, domestic cotton occupies an important position in the domestic market, while imported cotton from the United States and India is greatly squeezed out. The quantity of domestic cotton sold has also increased compared to previous years. Taking Shanghai alone, most of the raw cotton used by Chinese and Japanese textile mills is domestically produced, and the sales of imported cotton from the United States and India are not as good as before. The various figures are listed below for comparison.

Quantity of Raw Cotton Purchased by Chinese and Japanese Textile Mills in Shanghai

Type 1933 1934

Chinese Cotton 443,727 513,826

Tianjin American Cotton 12,230 17,876

Shandong Cotton 17,508 13,346

American Cotton 117,827 47,600

Indian Cotton 125,850 63,026

Egyptian Cotton 10,250 5,900

Total 697,652 630,354

Judging from the above table, although the total amount of cotton purchased by various Chinese and Japanese textile mills in Shanghai this year (excluding the second half of December) is slightly lower than last year, domestic cotton accounts for the highest percentage of raw cotton from all countries. Out of the total demand of 630,000 bales, Chinese cotton accounts for over 513,000 bales, or over 75%. The output from the United States, India, Egypt, and others has been greatly reduced. American cotton has plummeted by 60% compared to last year, Indian cotton has decreased by about half, and Egypt is similar to India. Domestic cotton has made such progress this year, and if it can continue, all foreign cotton will undoubtedly abandon its position in China.

Preparations for the Federation of Chinese Factories

Site of the Shanghai South National Exhibition

Yesterday Also Issued a Notice to Factories Clarifying Rumors

Xin Xin News Agency reports: The Shanghai South National Goods Exhibition organized by the Federation of Chinese National Goods Manufacturers on Yongji Lane, Xizang Road, has been actively underway since its inception, sparing no effort. As the opening is scheduled for New Year's Day next year, and time is pressing, the association first measured the area of the exhibition site yesterday to plan the construction of the stands. Yesterday, a notice was issued to member manufacturers clarifying that the Shanghai South National Goods Exhibition is not jointly organized with the China National Goods Association. The details are as follows:

Site Plan According to Liu Zhongying, a member of the standing committee of the association, the exhibition site has been rented on vacant land at the entrance of Hengxing Lane, 16 Pu, measuring approximately 250 square zhang. It is planned to build 120 bamboo sheds, each estimated to be one square zhang in depth and width. The main entrance of the exhibition site will be located on both the inner and outer roads. Four pedestrian walkways, each twelve feet wide, will be opened in the center of the site, and the perimeter will be connected to allow passage to the inner and outer roads. One pedestrian walkway at the main entrance and in the center of the site will be sixteen feet wide, allowing visitors to tour the site without getting confused. Inside the exhibition site, there will be an exhibition area where the products of various factories will be displayed in wooden-framed glass display cases. A lecture stage will be set up in the center of the exhibition area, and experts will be hired to give lectures on the theory of national goods every day. The office will be located in the northern part of the exhibition area, and the fire brigade and public team will be located at the main entrance in the north. Fire extinguishers will be widely hung throughout the site by the association's member factory, China Industrial Society, to supplement the fire brigade's efforts and ensure complete safety. As for the various projects, the site was measured and drawn yesterday, and an application has been submitted to the Public Works Bureau for a license. Construction of the site will begin immediately.

Notice of Clarification: Notice is hereby given that the association's Shanghai South National Goods Exhibition has been filed with the Municipal Party Department and the Social Affairs Bureau in accordance with the law, and preparations have been actively underway. However, yesterday, Fengchang Hosiery Factory and others came to the association, stating that the China National Goods Association had already collected booth fees from the factory and others. Hearing that the association was in the process of organizing the (Shanghai South National Goods Exhibition), they came to the association to inquire about the truth. In this regard, the association has never jointly organized any national goods exhibitions with any organization, except for those held in other provinces that were assisted by local authorities. The current national goods exhibition in Shanghai South is entirely organized and managed by the association alone. The claim of joint organization with the China National Goods Association is a rumor spread by someone with other motives. In addition to clarifying the matter to Fengchang Hosiery Factory and others, the association is concerned that members may be unaware of the truth and be deceived. Therefore, this notice is solemnly issued for your information.

Taifeng Company Closes Down

Affected by Huaming Match Factory

Guowen News Agency reports that Taifeng Canned Food Co., Ltd., has been operating in Shanghai for 29 years. In addition to the Nanjing Road main store and wholesale department, it has its own factory at 1501 Xiaoshadu Lane for manufacturing. The company has now been affected by Huaming Xingji Match Company and has hired accountant Xu Yongzuo and lawyer Zhang Zhengxue to declare bankruptcy. Details are as follows:

Taifeng's History All matters of Taifeng Company are the responsibility of directors Deng Ruiren, Huang Chuzhen, Tang Yinghua, Tang Yaojian, and Li Chongkun. The general manager is Wang Baru and the deputy manager is Fei Chuzhen. The factory manager is Deng Ruiren. The initial capital at the time of establishment was only 100,000 yuan. Later, due to business development, the capital was increased twice by 100,000 yuan, and now the total capital is 300,000 yuan.

Business Situation The company's main store is located at 255 Nanjing Road and has more than 90 employees. The wholesale department is attached to the main store. The Xiaoshadu Road factory is located on the banks of the Suzhou River and has more than 130 workers. Together with the senior office staff in the factory, there are approximately 240 to 250 people. The factory is divided into four departments: machine biscuits, meat, white iron. Manufacturing has been suspended since yesterday. A notice jointly signed by the accountant and lawyer is posted in front of the factory gate. Most of the workers are from Guangdong and have been working in the factory for more than ten years, with some reaching more than twenty years.

Reasons for Liquidation According to the staff of the main store, Taifeng has had profits every year. This closure is sudden and is entirely due to being affected by the Huaming Match Company. As for Huaming, it was established on Jiangwan Sports Club Road with an initial capital of 30,000 yuan. Due to losses, it was increased to 50,000 yuan. As business continued to be poor, the capital was further increased to 80,000 yuan. After several reorganizations, the total capital is now more than 100,000 yuan. The biggest reason for the failure of manager Su Yupeng and deputy manager Cai Keming is that Huaming was recently involved in a lawsuit over stamp tax issues, which cost a lot. The failure of Huaming's business led to Taifeng's inability to circulate funds and a sudden closure.

Consultations on the Aftermath The board of directors convened a meeting yesterday. All of Huaming's assets are now in the custody of Taifeng. The total amount owed to Taifeng is more than 400,000 yuan. If Huaming can be sold immediately to repay Taifeng, Taifeng can still reopen. However, liquidation is currently underway, and it is not easy to sell. Even if Taifeng wants to regroup, it will take time. (All notices from accountants and lawyers have appeared in advertisements and will not be recorded separately).

Pretending to Be an Uncle to Obtain Inheritance

Nephew and Uncle Had No Contact During Their Lives

No Evidence of Property in Court

The Nanshi District Court tried a case of inheritance claim a few days ago, the circumstances of which were quite interesting. The testimony is recorded below. A woman from Tongzhou, Chen Cao, 60 years old, currently residing in Caoxie Bay, Nanshi, runs a rickshaw house and owns 17 rickshaws, which bring in a decent income. Recently, Jiang Shengfa, through lawyer Gu Zukuan, filed a lawsuit with the district court to claim the inheritance of his uncle Jiang Jianqun, stating that his uncle had been living with Chen Cao for 16 years and opened a rickshaw company with 40 rickshaws. He also owned 30 to 40 mu of land in his hometown. His uncle recently died of illness, and his inheritance should be inherited by the petitioner. A few days ago, Jiang Shengfa was summoned to testify about the previous situation. Chen Cao testified that her late husband, Chen Meiming, had worked hard and frugally to open a rickshaw house and purchase 17 rickshaws, which he rented out for a living for more than 30 years. Ten years ago, he hired Jiang Jianqun as a partner to repair vehicles. Because Jiang was old and had been ill for several years, she treated him out of consideration for his years of partnership and because he was alone. He was treated by doctors but to no avail and died in September. The cost of his clothing and coffin was not insignificant. Unexpectedly, Jiang Shengfa suddenly appeared, falsely claiming to be the dead man's uncle, in an attempt to obtain the inheritance. This is ridiculous and should be rejected. The judge asked Jiang Shengfa, "What qualifications do you have to claim the inheritance?" Jiang replied, "My uncle had no heirs, so all the inheritance should be inherited by me." The judge said, "Chen Cao claims that it is the property of her husband. Do you have any proof?" Jiang answered, "No." Chen Cao said, "If he is Jiang Jianqun's nephew, why did he never visit him when he was alive? This shows that he is falsely claiming the relationship." The judge, after learning the situation, considered it unreasonable and reprimanded Jiang Shengfa in court, ordering him to leave. It is truly a curious tale.

Laborer Ma Rushan Chops Off Foreman's Left Arm

Dismissal Suspected to Be Masterminded

Principal Offender Arrested and Taken to the Bureau

Dong Zhan'ao, a 47-year-old Hebei native residing in No. 40, Zhoujiaqiao, West Shanghai, worked as a foreman in the sawmill on the north bank of the town. He was honest and amiable. However, Ma Rushan, a 22-year-old Hebei native and laborer in the factory, was dismissed a few days ago for beating people without reason in the factory. Ma falsely accused Dong of masterminding the dismissal and harbored deep resentment.

Yesterday at 9:00 AM, Ma gathered several accomplices and waited outside the factory, surrounding Dong to argue. They disagreed, and Ma led the crowd to attack, pulling out a sharp axe and chopping Dong several times. Dong was injured and fell to the ground, bleeding profusely. His left arm was chopped off, and his back was also chopped once. He fainted from the pain. Officer Wei of the police station at that location heard the alarm and rushed to the scene. The police arrested the assailant Ma Rushan, while the others fled. The injured man was immediately sent to the hospital for treatment. Ma Rushan and the axe were taken to the Caojiadu Branch Bureau. After questioning by Officer Liu, he was ordered to be taken to the bureau for further questioning.

Husband Stabs Adulterer to Death

Suspect Comes Face to Face

Arrested on the Spot

He Shifa, a 36-year-old Nanjing native, works as a butler in the home of a Russian at No. 10, Lane 327, Fuli Road, French Concession. He lives with his wife, Geng, a 36-year-old Nanjing native, at No. 137, Julai Road. He is fond of women and recently became involved with Liu Yang, the wife of Liu Baoyou (29 years old), a Xuzhou native who works in a Western store at No. 29, Maggie Road. When Liu is away from home, He goes to Liu's house to meet with Yang. At 1:30 AM the night before last, He finished his business and went to Liu's house to meet with Yang again. Liu Baoyou returned home unexpectedly and caught them in the act. Overwhelmed with jealousy, Liu grabbed He and beat him, stabbing He's head several times with a small knife and striking He's head with a small iron hammer, causing He to collapse unconscious. Liu then said to his wife, "Quickly hire a car to send him to the hospital for treatment. I'll go report to the police." He then escaped. Liu Yang followed her husband's instructions and sent He to the Red Cross Hospital on Haige Road. The hospital learned about He's injuries and reported it to the French police, who sent detectives to arrest Yang. He Shifa died at 10:20 PM that night due to severe head injuries. The hospital notified the police, who sent detectives to transport the body to the Tongren Funeral Home for an autopsy. They also went to Liu's home and took an iron hammer used in the attack. The murder weapon has not been found. Yesterday, He Geng, the wife of the deceased, and Zhang Hailong, the landlord of Liu Baoyou, were summoned to the police station. The case was reported to the Second Special Court. Prosecutor Wang Ren and forensic doctors Wei and Jiang, along with clerk Peng, arrived at the funeral home at noon to confirm that the deceased died from head injuries caused by an iron weapon. After questioning the deceased's wife and witnesses, they ordered the body to be handed over to the deceased's wife for burial, pending the police department's investigation and arrest of the suspect. Yesterday morning at approximately 10:00 AM, detectives took Liu Yang out to investigate the suspect. While walking along the intersection of Haige Road and Shanzhong Road, they encountered the suspect Liu Baoyou coming towards them. The detectives arrested him and took him to the police station to await interrogation by the court.

Continental Ship Destroys Sailboat

Waiting for Shipowner to Telegraph the Truth

The Continental Ship of Continental Industries Co., Ltd. at 20 Sijing Road, left Shanghai on the 18th, first arriving at Shantou to unload cargo, and then proceeding to Bangkok, Siam, to transport rice. After leaving port, the ship sailed to the outer waters of Wusong, where it encountered a sailboat, which it destroyed due to fog. Fortunately, the sailors were unharmed. After the incident, the Continental Ship owner reported to the Shanghai headquarters by wireless telegraph, stating only that the sailboat had been destroyed, without reporting the details. Continental Company then notified the Jianghai Customs Port Director, requesting him to investigate the details. The company also telegraphed the captain of the Continental Ship, ordering him to submit a detailed report for verification. Last night, according to the company, the captain's report had not arrived, but a letter had been sent to the Insurance Federation. After the shipowner's telegram arrives, a copy will be sent. The amount of the loss is not yet known for certain.

Currently Auditing Accounts

Since the Yong'an Silver Company temporarily suspended operations, there have been various rumors regarding the resumption of business. The reason for the company's suspension of operations was solely due to Ou Jiancheng's absconding with funds and unilaterally ordering the suspension of operations. Ou Jiancheng had centralized control over all departments of the company. Accountant Jiang is working day and night to expedite the audit. Once the audit is completed, the company will resume operations as soon as possible.

Bank of China and Shanghai Banks Handling Agricultural Loans in Shandong Province

Divided into Three Items: Tobacco, Cotton, and Silk

China has Implemented Shanghai Negotiations

Shanghai Bank Deputy Manager Zou Bingwen, for the bank's investment in Shandong Province to revive the rural economy, went to Jinan to negotiate loan methods with Shandong Province Chairman Han Fuju and Construction Department Director Zhang Honglie. He has now returned to Shanghai. According to the Xinsheng News Agency reporter, Shanghai Bank's loans to Shandong Province's agriculture are divided into three items: tobacco, cotton, and silk. Detailed methods are still being negotiated. After an agreement is reached, a contract will be signed, and it will be implemented next year. At the same time, the bank will guide rural areas to organize various cooperative societies for implementation. In addition, the Bank of China has already implemented the above three loan items in the province, with a total loan amount reaching 300,000 yuan.

City Center Department Store to Open on New Year's Day

Exclusively Selling Domestic Goods to Plug Leaks

To Provide Residents with Necessary Supplies

Since the municipal government moved to the city center this January, various facilities have been actively underway. A considerable number of citizens have rented or purchased houses and moved in. However, it is not very convenient to purchase daily necessities. Li Dachao, Jia Botao, Xu Shao, Tang Jinbai, Zhu Weiju, Mei Xinru, and others, in order to promote the prosperity of the city center and the convenience of the residents, organized a City Center Department Store Co., Ltd. and registered with the government. It is said that they have received the support of President Yu Youren, Mayor Wu Tiecheng, and various bureau directors of the municipal government, as well as famous people in the business and news communities. The company address has been selected in the city center area of ​​Shiguang Road and Minxian Road, where buildings have been constructed and everything is being installed. The main focus of the goods sold will be domestic daily necessities. The internal departments include twelve sections such as food, southern goods, candy, Chinese cuisine, Western cuisine, cosmetics, hardware, groceries, exchange services, machine weaving, and stationery. In addition to those who have already been selected, the remaining staff of each section will be introduced and examined by the China Vocational Education Society. It is also said that a notice will be published in the newspaper soon to solicit samples from domestic goods manufacturers in order to purchase and sell them. The company has set up an office at No. 23, Zhenping Lane, Songshan Road, French Concession, for the convenience of all parties. It is also said that the company has decided to open on New Year's Day next year.

Registration Date for Rickshaw Pullers in the French Concession

The Vehicle Affairs Department of the French Municipal Council announced yesterday that the registration of rickshaw pullers hired by private individuals will begin on January 2 next year. The owners of private rickshaw licenses must bring the rickshaw pullers to No. 23, Xuehuali Road, for registration. Registration forms can be obtained from various police stations in the French Concession. Registrations from January 2 to 5 will be limited to license numbers 1 to 750. From January 7 to 12, the limit will be license numbers 751 to 2,000. From January 14 to 19, the limit will be license numbers 2,001 to 3,000. From January 21 to 26, the limit will be license numbers 3,001 to 4,000. The vehicle license will only be issued by the Donations Department after the vehicle has been registered by the Vehicle Affairs Department. Starting in January, the vehicle license will be issued by the office at No. 28, Xuehuali Road.

Central and Southern China Cultural Association

Publishing the Monthly Magazine "Central and Southern China Culture"

The Central and Southern China Cultural Association, organized by comrades who study Southeast Asian issues in our country, aims to promote cultural exchange between China and Southeast Asia. Since its establishment, the association has been actively carrying out its affairs. To further its work, it has specially compiled and published the monthly magazine "Central and Southern China Culture." The inaugural issue has now been released, containing rich content contributed by Chen Zongshan, Zhou Qigang, Liu Shimu, Li Changfu, Gu Yinming, Huang Kangtun, Huang Sufeng, Xu Zhigui, Deng Zhibing, Wang Danhua, and others, all of whom are contemporary scholars studying Southeast Asian issues. It is an excellent resource for both domestic and international research on Southeast Asian immigration issues. Each issue is priced at 25 cents. The distribution office is located at No. 1358 Longhua Road, Shanghai, at the Central and Southern China Cultural Association Publishing Department. The Shanghai general sales agent is the Huiwen Bookstore at No. 180 Henan Road. Major bookstores in various cities also serve as sales agents.

Fire at Gongping Road

Yesterday morning around 6:00 AM, a fire broke out at a residence with the surname "Mou" at No. 15, Lane 446, at the intersection of Gongping Road and Seward Road in Hongkou. The fire was caused by a kerosene stove igniting improperly, setting the kerosene ablaze, which then ignited a mosquito net. Instantly, smoke and flames filled the air, making it impossible to approach. Fortunately, it was daytime, and residents were able to draw water and extinguish the fire. Only a bed curtain was burned, averting a major disaster. By the time the fire brigade arrived with its hose cart, the smoke had already cleared. It was indeed fortunate.

Gambling Den Cracked Down in a Teahouse on Tangqiao Street, Pudong

Gambling Boss Wang Hutu and 15 Others

Gambling paraphernalia delivered to the central station for interrogation yesterday.

Wu Tiecheng, the Mayor of Shanghai and concurrently the Director of the Public Security Bureau, received a confidential report that Wang Meigen (nickname Wang Hutu) from Wuxi, had secretly established a large gambling den in the third section of a teahouse at No. 643 Tangqiao Street, Pudong. He had gathered accomplices, including gamblers Chen Jinzhi and Shao Zhengxing from Nanjing, and Wu Amao from Changzhou, to entice ignorant villagers from the vicinity to gamble. Using pai gow and dice, they gambled day and night, making huge profits for Wang and his gang, who shared the spoils. Wu immediately ordered Lu Ying, the captain of the detective squad under the Pudong branch of the Public Security Bureau, to assign detective leaders Li Xiaobao and Chen Jinshan to investigate. Upon learning of this, Leader Li reported to Zhang Wuqin, the director of the Pudong branch, and led detectives including Li Guisheng and others, along with police officers from the Tangqiao Police Station, to the address on the date specified. They apprehended the boss Wang Meigen (Wang Hutu) on the spot, along with gambling suspects Yang Changshan, Wang Hexian, Du Xiangting, Wang Wenbin, Sun Jianmin, Zhang Fu, Chen Jinzhi, Shao Zhengxing, Xi Amao, Ma Zhangnan, Xu Rongsheng, Min Ajin, Qu Yongsheng, Gao Futang, and others, totaling fifteen people. They also seized gambling equipment such as pai gow tiles, dice, chips, and gambling funds. All the suspects were taken to the central police station. After interrogation by Captain Lu, they were handed over to the Third Section of the Public Security Bureau for legal action yesterday.

Robbery Case at a Brick and Tile Store in Pudong

Three Robbers Apprehended

Delivered to the Central Station for legal proceedings yesterday.

The Jiang Shengyi brick and tile store in Lujia Duhan, South Pudong, was robbed of valuables on November 7th. The case was reported to Yang Zhongquan, the head of the Yangjiadu Police Station in Pudong, under the Municipal Public Security Bureau. He ordered his subordinates to investigate and apprehend the robbers. It was learned that the criminals were hiding in a certain location. Director Yang and his team including police inspectors and officers disguised themselves and secretly raided the hideout on the date specified. They captured local robbers Wei Zhonggen and Zhu Lan, along with Dong Yougen, who was harboring stolen goods. During the interrogation, the suspects confessed to the armed robbery. Director Li prepared a written statement and handed over the suspects to the Central Bureau for legal action.

Assaulted for Seeking Unpaid Wages

Fang Zhongda Fined Thirty Yuan

Xu Li, a woman from Taicang residing at No. 9 Tongfeng Lane, Dapuqiao, Jin Shenfu Road, French Concession, went to the Sanxin Knitting Factory at No. 43 in the same lane on the 15th of this month to collect her wages. However, Fang Zhongda, the factory manager, not only refused to pay but also assaulted her without reason, causing injuries to her face and other areas. Ms. Li reported the incident to the French Concession Police, requesting an investigation. The police agreed and dispatched detectives to arrest Fang. He was then handed over to the Eighth Criminal Court of the Second Special District Court. After hearing the case, the court ordered Fang to post bail pending further investigation of the victim's injuries. During the subsequent hearing yesterday, Xu Li testified about the assault and injuries she sustained. Fang Zhongda claimed that the plaintiff had come to demand wages from the foreman Shen Genxi, and they had argued. He said that he asked them to go outside to talk and did not assault her. The witness Shen Genxi testified that Ms. Li had come to demand 3,000 wen in wages because she had overdrawn too much. He refused to pay, leading to an argument. The manager told them to go outside to talk. Ms. Li tripped and fell on the threshold, injuring herself, but the manager did not strike her. Judge Sun Peng, after reviewing the evidence, stated that the victim's injuries had been certified by a forensic doctor, and there was no room for denial. Therefore, the court sentenced Fang Zhongda to a fine of thirty yuan for assault.

Qingxiao Society Recruiting Members

Effective from New Year's Day

The Chinese Qingxiao Society at No. 199 Taixing Road, Wusong, has been expanding its organization.

Since its expansion, the internal structure has become increasingly sound, attracting the attention of social figures. The society's main goal is to study the essence of Chinese literature and hold monthly tests and competitions to seek new developments in education, resist the cultural aggression of foreign powers, promote China's inherent national ideology, and encourage national unity to assist the government. It has specially hired renowned scholars as advisors to ensure that the society's operations are well-guided. It is reported that the Basic Committee has resolved to launch a large-scale membership recruitment campaign starting on New Year's Day next year to fulfill the common desire to learn from each other and revive the national spirit. Detailed information can be obtained by sending two cents in postage to the society.

Abduction of a Young Girl Held Pending Judgment

A fifteen-year-old girl named A Bao, from Taizhou and residing at No. 6 Pingliang Road, was a worker at the Shanghai Cotton Mill on Guangxin Road. On the afternoon of the 15th of this month at around 6:00 PM, Zhao Songchen (also known as Xiao Chen), a twenty-two-year-old fellow villager, lured her to the rooftop of the New World Company to play and watch a performance. Later, he tricked her into staying overnight at the home of a friend surnamed Jin in Caojiadu, Huajie. After his daughter went missing, her father, Sun Wensheng, searched for her without success. He reported the incident to the Yangshupu Police Station. Until the day before yesterday, Mr. Jin notified the police station. Detectives were dispatched to arrest Zhao. Upon questioning, it was discovered that he and the girl were living in the Concession. The Jing'an Temple Police Station was informed and sent Chinese and foreign detectives to bring them back to the police station, then transferred to Yangshupu Police Station. The girl was returned to Sun Wensheng. Yesterday morning, Zhao was handed over to the Third Criminal Court of the First Special District Court. Mr. Li Zhishan, a lawyer from the Public Works Department, recounted the events. When questioned, the defendant stated that the girl did not want to go home and went with him to the home of his friend surnamed Jin in Caojiadu to stay temporarily. There was no improper conduct. Because Jin extorted him for ten yuan, he reported the incident to the police station. His other statements were evasive. The girl stated that she and Jin slept in the same bed at Jin's house, while he slept on another bed. Nothing else happened. Judge Wu Zehan ordered the defendant to be held pending sentencing on a later date.

Sentencing for Illegally Establishing a Morphine Injection Den

Gu Junyan, a Chinese detective from the Huishan Police Station, cracked down on a morphine injection den at No. 3010 Yuanfang Lane, East Broadway Road, on the afternoon of the 13th of this month at around 8:00 PM. The owner, Fang A San, from Tongzhou, was arrested along with customers Feng You, Wang A Bao, and others. Thirty-three packets of morphine and six needles were seized and taken to the police station. Mr. Li Zhishan, a lawyer from the Public Works Department of the First Special District Court, requested severe punishment. The court ordered all defendants to be held pending sentencing. Yesterday morning, Judge Wu Zehan presided over the Third Criminal Court and sentenced Fang A San to one year and six months in prison. A Bao was sentenced to fifty days of detention. Feng You, Xue San, and Xu Er were each sentenced to forty days of detention. The evidence was confiscated, and Ji Louchang was acquitted.

Wang Jiliu, a man from Jiangbei, 34 years old, committed suicide due to financial difficulties and inability to support himself. Yesterday afternoon at 4:00 PM, he hanged himself inside a wooden pavilion at the intersection of Meizhou Road and Hejian Road. A passerby reported the incident to the Yangshupu Police Station. Letter to the Editor

Esteemed Editor,

Having carefully read the news column of your esteemed newspaper on the third page concerning local news, which reported that Dr. Wang Zhenchuan was detained by the Garrison Headquarters, and that the reason for his arrest was suspected to be related to the drug case uncovered in Zhabei, and is currently under investigation by the military court, we are greatly surprised to find that this does not correspond with the facts. Our director has always been cautious and self-respecting, and would never engage in rash or unconventional behavior. His dedication to voluntary smoking cessation demonstrates his abhorrence of drugs. However, someone who once stayed at the hospital for treatment and owed hospital fees suddenly implicated him in an old case, claiming he knew about it, which is why he was summoned for questioning, not arrested. Furthermore, the claim that he is connected to some drug organization is purely unfounded. We believe your newspaper's report was based on misinformation. Therefore, we are writing this letter to request a correction, to clarify the truth. We would be extremely grateful. With respect,

Shanghai Jishan Hospital, December 20th.

The Xujiahui Observatory's weather forecast at 4:30 PM yesterday states that the Shandong area is cloudy and cold, with light and variable winds. The middle and lower reaches of the Yangtze River are partly cloudy, relatively cold, and conditions are unstable. There will be fog in the morning, with winds from the northeast to north. Essays

Little Western Paradise

— by Zhang Henshui

Chapter 6: A Poor Girl Cannot Be Forced to Teach, Viewing a Western Teacher as No More Than a Humble Heart

Jia Duocai smiled and said, "Can you really call these little guys guests? If a foreigner wants to come, I'll immediately send them packing. But I'm curious to know what these two foreigners are really after."

Li Shilian said, "Westerners' customs are different from Chinese people's. They won't engage in meaningless pleasantries. If they want to come, they must have a purpose. I think they must be asking you about the situation in the Northwest, to gather information for some research."

Jia Duocai said, "I bet they see me as a scholar, interviewing me about the economic situation in the Northwest. These Europeans and Americans are truly formidable; they won't even let someone ordinary like me, a banker, off the hook. Alright, tell them to come in an hour. Let me sit in the room and think quietly about how to phrase things. I have a systematic study on the cotton production in Shaanxi, which I can present to him."

Li Shilian said, "Okay, I'll go reply. I think they're genuinely sincere in visiting you. They'll come even if they have to wait an hour."

Jia Duocai said seriously, "It doesn't matter whether they come or not; I need to consider things before I meet them. You must understand that this is a matter related to the nation's dignity. We must make sure we don't make any mistakes in our words."

Li Shilian thought that there must be a reason for the foreigners' special visit. With Jia Duocai's embellishment, he felt it was even more unusual, and repeatedly said, "Yes, yes."

Jia Duocai returned to the room and immediately waved his hands at the Hu sisters, saying, "You can leave now; I'm having some foreigners come over."

Mrs. Hu asked, "Are they devils?"

Jia Duocai waved his hand again and said, "Go, go. We can talk about anything later."

Yueying had been subjected to several tens of minutes of examination in this room, and she felt wronged enough. Since Master Jia was dismissing people like this, it could be considered a lifeline for her. Why would she still sit here? She stood up first and walked out the door, followed by Mrs. Hu. (95)

Literary Anecdotes

— by Shayu

Red Bean Thoughts For that "Red beans grow in the South, this thing best evokes longing" red bean poem, "red bean" has become an elegant object in literary circles. Throughout history, countless poems and lyrics have praised red beans, such as Tang Dynasty poet Wen Tingyun's "Exquisite dice inlaid with red beans, knowing whether the longing reaches the bone"? These are all borrowed, like Wang Wei's, to symbolize longing. Mr. Qian Muqi of the Qing Dynasty had a red bean tree in front of his study, so he named his study "Red Bean Villa." Mr. Qian was a great Confucian scholar of his time, so the red beans of Changshu became famous throughout the South and were highly regarded by contemporaries. In fact, Anhui, Guangdong, and other provinces all produce them. Even the West Dongting Mountain, which belongs to Suzhou, has two red bean trees. Among the types of red beans, those produced on Zhubu Mountain in Anhui are the most lovable. The beans are about the size of yellow soybeans, oval in shape, and bright red in color. The longer they are worn, the brighter they become. Mr. Hanyun once gave two of these red beans to the respected father of Yu Yifen. Although the red beans of Changshu are famous because of people, their shape is about the size of Go stones, not perfectly round, and their color varies from red to black. Mr. Yu Youqing, a colleague of Tongwen, collected and entrusted stores to sell a large quantity of Changshu red beans this year. This aroused opposition from several people who had been storing red beans, who believed that Mr. Yu was selling love-sick beans as merchandise, which was too demeaning to such an elegant object. According to Mr. Yu, his sale of red beans was originally to raise funds for compiling a "Red Bean Poetry Collection." However, this has already caused a small dispute in Suzhou newspapers.

Fragrant Grass and Beautiful Woman Writers are, after all, sentimental souls. Ever since Qu Lingjun, the grand master of the Chu kingdom, created the term "fragrant grass and beautiful woman" in his poem "Li Sao," a group of writers have entrusted their deep emotions to famous flowers and fragrant grasses. For example, Tao Jingjie's love of chrysanthemums and Zhou Dunyi's love of lotuses are well-known and admired by later generations. Among modern writers who love flowers, Mr. Hu Shiyu's love of plum blossoms, Mr. Cheng Zhanlu's love of winter plum blossoms, and our editor Mr. Zhou's love of violets can also be considered fine anecdotes in the literary world.

Snippets

— (Hongxia)

According to statistics from the International Trade Bureau, in the past ten months, the total value of imported cosmetics and perfumes amounted to 1,451,788 national currency, an increase of 24,000 yuan compared to the same period last year. This number is truly alarming. If this huge sum is divided by ten months, the average daily expenditure would be 4,839.29 yuan. This sum of money is entirely consumed by women in bits and pieces of cosmetics and perfumes. Female compatriots, please do not belittle these small amounts of cosmetics and perfumes!

Records of My Fragrant Past

— Originally Written by Princess Der Ling of the Qing Dynasty, Translated by Qin Shouou

"If we find that your behavior has not improved by then, your second tail will have to be cut off!" The fox happily agreed, declaring that it was also aware of its faults and willing to try its best to reform. However, after returning, a thousand years quickly passed, and its behavior was still very bad. The only difference in the past thousand years was that it had never been drunk once; but its various bad habits continued to play out, and its misdeeds were obvious, no matter how cunning it was, it could not deny them. The Jade Emperor, of course, knew about this long ago, so he immediately grabbed it and cut off another tail. At the same time, hoping that it could reform, he gave it another thousand years, as before, to slowly turn over a new leaf. The fox also tearfully agreed. But after returning, it soon reverted to its old ways, indulging in wrongdoing. In the blink of an eye, the second millennium had passed, and the Jade Emperor carefully examined it. Apart from not having drunk alcohol and not having lied, it still had no good qualities. Its refusal to repent was, needless to say, very disappointing to the Jade Emperor, so he decided to continue to punish it. Fortunately, it still had seven tails! So, every thousand years, it was assessed once, and the result of each assessment was always unsatisfactory, so he cut off one tail each time. After eight thousand years, the fox had only one tail left, but its behavior was still not perfect. According to the Jade Emperor's intention, it could not keep this last tail either, so he grabbed it again, telling it that it could no longer be forgiven. This time, in order to remove the root of all evil, its last tail had to be cut off as well. Perhaps such a disposition would be able to transform it into a kind and docile fox. (205)

In Memory of Mr. Li Shicen

— Zhou Zheng

Mr. Li's death is undoubtedly a great loss to the academic community. In China, where scholars are scarce, it is especially worthy of our grief. Mr. Li was a philosopher. He first supported Nietzsche's theories, and then underwent several transformations, but he was always pursuing the truth. He believed that in order to escape suffering, one must first be able to endure pain, so he constantly persevered upwards.

Of course, in an era where scholars are commercialized, and there is jealousy and exclusion, he could not avoid being attacked and slandered by others. He was like a white candle, purely burning his own life. In the light of electric lamps, his own brilliance and greatness seemed invisible, but I firmly believe that temporary clouds cannot cover the clear sky for long.

His lectures, although he did not call roll, were always full, and there were often people who could not get seats and had to stand and listen, or sit on the podium next to the lectern. His sincere attitude and demeanor seemed to be the embodiment of truth. Anyone would be influenced by him. But he never had the deceit of a sophist; he had the demeanor of a pure scholar. Under the combined assault of depression and financial hardship, a perfect person in the academic world was sacrificed. What he left us is a passion, an infinitely strong force of truth. We should eliminate general academic peddlers and inherit Mr. Li's spirit of scholarship.

God's Masterpiece

— Yue

Iron Tree

— Yan Chonglou

"This is an iron tree. Although it looks like a section of dead wood now, it will sprout in the future." Last year, one day, a friend brought me something and said this to me.

I thanked him and took what he gave me. It was a section of dead tree that had been sawn off and planted in a ceramic pot.

"Iron tree? Can dead wood still sprout?" I listened to my friend's words, and my heart was full of suspicion. I casually put it in the corner of the room.

After that, I still watered it from time to time, but it didn't show any signs of sprouting.

This spring, I transplanted it from the pot to a small garden, intending to let it get more natural rain and dew. But it was still silent. I had almost completely given up hope of it sprouting.

Suddenly, one morning in the summer, I unintentionally discovered a tender sprout coming out next to this piece of dead wood. I was so surprised that I shouted out, "The iron tree can still come back to life after all!"

Now, this sprout has gradually grown into a small tree. Its lush green leaves are still as luxuriant as ever in this cold and windy weather.

"One should never despair of anything in the world," I thought.

This resurrected iron tree gave me the inspiration that "life must have a strong power." This iron tree gave me the symbol that "life must be fought to the end."

Acknowledgment: Dr. Huang Yizhao, a one-finger Chan Tuina massage doctor at No. 3, Lane 21, South Chengdu Road in this city, has a long family tradition and has cured many serious illnesses over the years. Recently, in order to promote the art of one-finger Chan medicine, Dr. Huang has compiled "Dr. Huang's Medical Tales," a book based on his experiences in clinical practice over the past decade, to send to all sectors. The book is rich in content and contains prefaces and inscriptions by important figures in the military, political, business, and academic circles. It is said that those who request it by mail only need to state their address and attach a four-cent stamp, and it will be sent as a gift.

Personality Sketches

Cheng Yaosheng and Hu Shi

— Zheng Yimei

The old painter Mr. Cheng Yaosheng has recently become the subject of social gossip due to an abandonment case. I was once a student under Mr. Cheng when he was teaching at Caoqiao Middle School in Wuzhong, so yesterday I visited him. The old gentleman looked very frail, and his eyes were blind. When a guest arrived, he had to call out his name to identify him. When I arrived, Mr. Cheng was very happy and recounted the lawsuit, saying that he was in a declining state in his old age and had encountered this unexpected storm. He said that the accusations were completely fabricated, which was something he never could have imagined. In short, he had always held the belief that blessings should not be enjoyed alone, and that if one was blessed by heaven, one should share it with others. However, those who did not understand him thought he had an abundance and possessed vast wealth, and therefore coveted it. In fact, he was in a poor situation, especially in recent years. Therefore, he never had two meat dishes for a meal and never had his own car to travel. Even all the utensils he used were bought cheaply from Beijing Road, mismatched and untidy. Upon inspection, the stools were broken, the table was damaged, and there was a jumble of clutter. There were absolutely no luxurious items. The most laughable thing was that one end of the painting table was still intact, while the other end was missing, so it was supported by two upright kerosene wooden boxes. On the table were several outdated photographs, leaving traces of his past glory, which were worth commemorating. I happened to notice a group photograph of teachers and students of the New China Public School. Hu Shi, the literary giant of today, was there. Mr. Yaosheng and he had been at the same school for many years and were very close. Shi had even written a poem for Mr. Yaosheng. I copied it down in pencil: "Knowing that Wu and Yue are in the same boat, but the raging waves shake the earth. Birds still circle the trees above the river, and the remaining butterflies before you have turned to ash. The fleeting epiphyllum leaves only regrets, and the lingering marks of wild geese are also pitiful. Do not laboriously make straw dogs, but discuss the flavor to the dark green moss." At that time, Shi had not yet engaged in the New Culture Movement, so his work still had a sharp, ornate rhyme.

Umeya Shokichi

— Qing Qu

The newspaper on November 20th carried a "Tokyo dispatch from Japan Alliance News Agency" stating that "Mr. Umeya Shokichi, a Japanese national who has a close relationship with the Chinese Revolution, is suffering from a stomach ulcer. He passed away at his villa in Chiba Prefecture on the 23rd. Mr. Umeya was a native of Nagasaki and went to Shanghai at the age of 23. He interacted with Sun Yat-sen and other key figures in the Chinese Revolution and made great contributions to the Chinese revolutionary cause." This part of history, now that Umeya has passed away, I am afraid very few people know the details. Therefore, I will write a few words about it. About five years ago, Umeya brought the portrait of the late Premier, which he had cast, and his family from Japan to our China, and personally went to the capital to pay homage to his spirit. He did not hesitate to travel a long distance, spending a huge amount of money, and all out of personal action. At first, everyone was a little strange. Perhaps some people still remember this matter! I don't know if Umeya was really an old friend of Mr. Zhongshan. As the historical record says, "True friendship is seen in life and death." Among the Japanese who have come to our China, no one, no matter who they are, can have a good impression of him. However, Umeya alone, I think, is impossible not to know about his loyal and chivalrous heart. Even when he and Mr. Zhongshan were socializing overseas, I am afraid that there was only this one person!

Umeya probably opened a photography studio around 1894 or 1895 at No. 8 Central Road, Hong Kong. His store was called "Umetani." Later, through the introduction of the Westerner Kang Deli, he became friends with Mr. Zhongshan. Mr. Zhongshan also felt very close to him, chatting with him day and night, sometimes until late at night, and staying at Umeya's place. Do you think they were close friends? When Mr. Zhongshan was in trouble and went to London, Umeya, although in Hong Kong, still entrusted a pastor named Ou Fengshi to secretly relay messages on his behalf. When he received the shocking news that Mr. Zhongshan was missing, he tried to find his whereabouts and prepared for him to escape to Japan. Therefore, at that time, Heiwa Heishū, Miyazaki Torazo (i.e., White Wave Raging Sky), and others all got to know Mr. Zhongshan. Even the progressive figures in the Min Party, like Inukai Tsuyoshi and others, also deeply believed in the Premier, all of which can be said to be due to Umeya's efforts in promoting him.

Mr. Zhongshan first wanted to go to Taiwan according to Chen Shaobai's suggestion. Umeya returned to Japan and strongly opposed it, thinking that "Taiwan belongs to the Manchus, and Japan is safer." Therefore, Mr. Zhongshan used the Zhongshan Marquis's residence as a temporary dwelling, calling himself "Zhongshan," and it became his name from then on. At that time, it coincided with the failure of the Reform Movement of 1898 in our country, and Kang and Liang also fled to Japan. Umeya mistakenly thought that they were also revolutionaries and could form comrades. Before long, Umeya regretted his difficulty in recognizing people in front of Mr. Zhongshan. I still remember that Mr. Zhongshan gave a speech somewhere in Shanghai, which he personally spoke about. Now that I see the news of Umeya's death in the newspaper, I wrote this article.

Education News

Banning Students from Entering Dance Halls

Universities Should Take Multiple Approaches

Presidents and Faculty Should Lead by Example by Abstaining from Dance Halls

Promote Wholesome Entertainment to Divert Students' Impulses

Students Must Wear Uniforms at All Times for Identification

The Municipal Education Bureau Sent a Notice to Universities Yesterday

The Shanghai Municipal Education Bureau yesterday sent a notice to all public and private universities in the city regarding the ban on university students entering dance halls, citing Ordinance No. 11658 from the Municipal Government, which stated: "Referring to the letter from the Shanghai University Federation stating, 'Respectfully, the Federation passed a resolution at its third executive committee meeting on October 27 to ban students from entering dance halls. The Federation has written to the Municipal Government to request that it find a way to investigate and notify the original schools at any time, and that the Federation will send a notice to all schools to strictly enforce the ban and immediately expel such students.' As dance halls abound in Shanghai, students from various schools often easily enter dance halls, leading to the moral corruption of young people, not only neglecting their studies but also causing lifelong harm. The Federation deeply sympathizes with this. Now that the New Life Movement is about to be implemented, it is noted that various countries in the East and West have precedents for banning students from entering dance halls, and the dance halls have announced that they do not accept students. Therefore, we are writing to your esteemed government to find a way to investigate and notify the original schools at any time to expel them immediately, which will greatly benefit the future of education. This is an order to investigate and report back.' Upon receipt of this, it is noted that the majority of dance halls in the city are located in the concessions. In addition to having the Bureau submit a request to the Municipal Government to consult with the authorities of the First and Second Special Districts to order all dance halls within the special districts not to admit students for dancing, the Boards of Directors of the various special districts should also send personnel to jointly investigate and prohibit with the personnel sent by the Bureau to the various dance halls in person. If students are found dancing in the halls, the school they belong to will be identified, notified to expel them, and notified to all schools not to allow them to transfer. Furthermore, the major middle schools in the city should be ordered to strictly restrain the students in school, provide constant guidance, explain the great principles, and make clear the advantages and disadvantages. The presidents and faculty of each school should especially lead by example, abstaining from dance halls to be a practical model. Friendly venues should be urgently established within the schools, educational films should be screened, wholesome entertainment should be promoted, and strict military training should be implemented to divert students' impulses and regulate their weary bodies and minds. Students must wear uniforms at all times, whether in or out of school, for identification and may not wear other clothing. The schools should find ways to contact the families of the students, notify them of the situation at any time to provide mutual assistance, and encourage students to supervise each other. If any abnormal behavior is discovered, it should be reported to the teachers for investigation and punishment. With both sides working together, it should be easier to salvage the situation. In addition to reporting back at any time for verification, the corresponding notice is sent to your esteemed school, hoping that you will investigate and implement it and reply accordingly."

Full Text of the Resolutions of the National Vocational Education Conference (3)

Article 12 Regarding Vocational School Curriculum

The Industrial Vocational Department should add courses on the overview of the industry and factory design (proposed by Wei Yuanguang).

Resolution Adopt the original proposal: "Add an industrial overview course in the second year and a factory design course in the graduation year (the content and complexity of the teaching materials can be changed according to the differences in junior, senior, and the nature of the industry)," and pay attention to the third method in the general explanation on page 109 of the Compilation of Vocational Education Laws and Regulations: "Among vocational subjects, there should be subjects on the enterprise, management, administration, and all practical economics of the profession being studied."

Please compile and print textbooks for general subjects in vocational schools to facilitate students' progress (proposed by the Fujian Provincial Department of Education).

Please the Ministry of Education to specifically compile a "Citizenship Textbook" for vocational schools to strengthen students' commitment to their professions (proposed by the Sichuan Provincial Department of Education).

(The above two proposals were discussed together)

Resolution Please the Ministry of Education to collect current textbooks from vocational schools across the country, and then entrust research vocational education institutions or experts to review and compile textbooks for general subjects and citizenship textbooks in vocational schools.

Determine the syllabus for vocational subjects in private and labor schools (proposed by the Shanghai Municipal Education Bureau).

Resolution Send to the Ministry of Education for reference.

Vocational schools should add elective subjects in addition to the prescribed general subjects, and order local schools to increase them as appropriate (proposed by the Henan Provincial Department of Education).

Resolution Vocational schools may add general subjects closely related to the department, not exceeding three hours and without hindering the department's main subjects.

Article 13 Regarding Vocational Supplementary Education

Promote vocational supplementary education (proposed by the Ministry of Education).

Please order each province and city to vigorously implement vocational supplementary education (proposed by the Fujian Provincial Department of Education).

Resolution 1. The Ministry of Education and the Ministry of Industry should find ways to promote labor education laws and regulations and order each province and city to order local agricultural, commercial, and industrial groups to set up vocational supplementary education institutions within a limited time to allow apprentices from factories and stores to enroll in supplementary education.

2. Local educational administrative agencies should contact local agricultural, commercial, and industrial sectors to set up various vocational schools or supplementary schools within a limited time.

3. Local educational administrative agencies may contact local agricultural, commercial, and industrial sectors to organize a vocational supplementary education design committee.

4. Please the Ministry of Education to issue a notice to each province and city, directing them to pay attention to running vocational supplementary schools under the social education funding.

Article 14 Regarding Vocational Guidance

Vocational guidance should be vigorously implemented in primary and secondary schools (proposed by the Ministry of Education).

Resolution

1. The personnel in charge of vocational guidance in primary and secondary schools in each province and city should order all primary and secondary schools in the province and city to vigorously implement vocational guidance within one academic year before students graduate.

2. Educational administrative agencies in each province and city should hire experts and leaders from various industries to organize vocational guidance committees and advisory boards.

3. Educational administrative agencies in each province and city should hold vocational guidance holiday workshops on a regular basis.

4. Local educational administrative agencies should conduct a survey of the overall vocational situation in the province and city and publish vocational analysis booklets for distribution to schools.

5. Local educational administrative agencies should set up vocational guidance centers or job placement agencies within the shortest possible time.

6. The Ministry of Education is requested to issue a notice to the educational administrative agencies of each province and city to earnestly comply with the above five methods.

7. Please the Ministry of Education to establish a summer vocational guidance workshop to convene people in charge of vocational guidance from each province and city to participate.

Temporary Proposal Please formulate methods for cultivating vocational education in elementary schools to popularize vocational education

(Proposed by Jiang Wenyu)

Resolution The original proposal is sent to the Ministry of Education for reference, and the Ministry is requested to formulate detailed methods for implementation. (End)

Ministry of Education Orders to All Provinces and Cities

Prepare for Centralized Military Training

Barracks and Equipment

Yesterday, the Ministry of Education approved a request from the General Directorate of Training to instruct the education departments and bureaus of all provinces and cities to uniformly concentrate high school and equivalent school students for three months of military training, starting in April of next year. Each province and city should consult with the local National Military Training Committee to prepare barracks and equipment early. The original order stated:

"The General Directorate of Training's request stated that Article 22 of the revised school military education plan stipulates, 'Centralized barracks will be designated by the provincial and municipal governments. If repairs or additions are needed, the expenses will be paid by the provincial and municipal governments. Wooden utensils will also be procured by the provincial and municipal governments.' It is hereby ordered that centralized training for high school and equivalent school students will commence in April of next year, as previously decreed. The date is fast approaching. All provincial and municipal governments should prepare in advance to avoid being caught off guard at the last minute. In addition to presenting this matter to Chairman Chiang of the Military Affairs Commission, who approved an order to the eleven provincial governments of Jiangsu, Zhejiang, Anhui, Jiangxi, Hubei, Hunan, Henan, Hebei, Shandong, Fujian, and Yunnan, as well as the four municipal governments of Nanjing, Shanghai, Beiping, and Qingdao, to expedite preparations by the newly established National Military Training Committee, a corresponding communication will be sent to the military training committees of each province and city. Please investigate, instruct, consult, and handle this matter with utmost diligence.' Therefore, in addition to issuing separate orders, this order is hereby issued for your information and compliance."

Request for One Million Education Funds Under Review

The Henan Education Staff Association telegraphed the Executive Yuan on the 12th of this month, stating that the reduction in deed tax revenue in Henan Province has severely strained education funding, requesting an annual allocation of one million yuan from salt tax revenue or other taxes. The Executive Yuan has now instructed the Ministries of Finance and Education to discuss and respond for review and action.

The joint meeting of the Boxer Indemnity Fund organization was held at the Executive Yuan on the 20th. Shanghai Branch Discusses Education System Issues

Members Express Detailed Opinions

After Consolidation, a Decision Will Be Submitted to the Ministry of Education for Consideration

The Shanghai branch of the China Education Society held its 13th membership meeting yesterday afternoon at 6:00 PM at the Eight Immortals Bridge YMCA. Attendees included Zheng Xigu, Chen Xuan'shan, Zhang Zhonghuan, Shu Xincheng, Zeng Zuozhong, Zhang Yaoxiang, Zhang Yousan, Liao Maoru, Yang Weiyu, Ou Yuanhuai, Mao Yanwen, Shen Tilan, and others, totaling several dozen people. The members all expressed detailed opinions on this issue, lasting for quite some time. Finally, four points of consensus were reached, and a decision was made to submit them to the Ministry of Education for consideration. The documents are currently being organized by the clerk and will be sent to the members for review before being published for clarity and accuracy.

Northeast Education Relief Agency

Deadline for Subsidies to Needy Northeast Students

Letter from the Municipal Education Bureau Relaying Instructions to All Schools

Applications Received After the Deadline Will Be Held Over for the Next Term

The Northeast Youth Education Relief Agency sent a letter to the Shanghai Municipal Education Bureau stating that the agency's methods for subsidizing needy students from the Northeast, along with endorsement forms, have already been sent for distribution to the subordinate secondary schools for thorough investigation. Needy students from the Northeast currently studying should submit endorsements within fifteen days of receiving the documents, in accordance with the procedures, for review and processing. The letter states that the aforementioned deadline has already passed, and some schools have not been able to submit applications on time due to procedural issues. The agency has difficulty compiling and reviewing the cases. Therefore, a deadline has been set for receiving endorsement forms for this term. All schools and universities in Beiping must submit applications by October 10th, and all other schools and universities in other provinces and cities must submit applications by December 15th. Applications received after the deadline will be held over for the next term. In addition to publishing a notice, a corresponding letter is sent for your information and dissemination.

Fudan University High School

Record of the Dedication Ceremony of Li Xue Tang

Fudan University High School, affiliated with Xujiahui, built Li Xue Tang in memory of Mr. Shao Lizi and his wife, Ms. Fu Xuewen, for their contribution to supporting the high school, to commemorate their contributions. The school held the dedication ceremony at 10:00 AM yesterday. Guests and alumni present included Chairman Shao Lizi, Ms. Fu Xuewen, Director Pan Gongzhan, representatives from the Shanghai University Faculty Union Chen Gaoyong, President Cao Liangxia of Datong University, Secretary-General Jin Tongyin of Fudan University, Dean Yu Nanqiu of the College of Liberal Arts, representative of the Board of Directors Zhu Zhonghua, representative of the Alumni Association Wang Sifang, as well as alumni Shao Shizhou, Ye Jichun, Ye Zaoting, Gu Yinming, He Youmei, Shao Suichu, and all faculty and students of the affiliated high school, totaling over 700 people. The ceremony was conducted with proper etiquette. First, Principal Li Denghui delivered the opening remarks, followed by Director Yin Yiwen reporting on the construction of the new building. Then, Mr. and Mrs. Shao unveiled the plaque and opened the doors, with cannons fired and music played. The ceremony was very grand. Immediately after, speeches were given, with much humility and briefly recounting the history of the affiliated high school. The meaning of the two characters Li Xue (endeavor and learning) was explained to encourage the students. Director Pan then spoke, praising the school's long history and offering much encouragement and exhortation. The ceremony concluded at about 11:00 AM, after which Principal Li and Director Yin accompanied Mr. and Mrs. Shao, Director Pan, and other guests on a tour of the classrooms and dormitories. Each classroom was uniquely decorated by the students with great ingenuity, filled with a dazzling array of beautiful items. The dormitories were also very clean and tidy. At 11:30 AM, a review was held, with the students' lines orderly and their spirits high, which was highly commended. The student army also performed field exercises, and the Boy Scouts performed bridge building, flag signaling, and so on. For a time, cannons roared, and hand-thrown grenades were launched simultaneously, with smoke filling the air and a thunderous sound, almost as if on a battlefield. At 12:30 PM, everyone gathered at the Boy Scout headquarters for a meal. In the afternoon, the alumni, faculty, and all students competed in basketball and various games, with cheers resounding throughout. At about 3:00 PM, the entertainment began, with a variety of programs, including songs and dances by Fudan Elementary School and Fudan Charity Elementary School, as well as dramas and music by students from both the senior and junior high school departments. Mr. and Mrs. Shao lingered until 4:00 PM before leaving the school. In the evening, the school's students had a dress rehearsal of Peking Opera, with the female student Ye Cuiying and Shi Kuangzhuang, Zhi Jin, Zhang Dianquan, Fa Jiakan, and others performing brilliantly in "Female Escort," "Cosmic Madness," "Empty City Stratagem," and "Picking Up Gold." The festivities ended joyfully at 1:00 AM.

Shen Yuan Middle School Sports Federation Soccer Match

Bloody Tragedy Occurs

Yuqing Wins 3-1 Over Jinan

Result of the Attack: Six Yuqing Players Seriously Injured

The Xie Jin Hui Office Was Smashed

In the Shanghai Middle School Sports Federation soccer competition, Jinan High School and Yuqing Middle School had equal scores in the "Shang" group. A final match was held yesterday afternoon at 3:00 PM at Shen Yuan to determine the winner of this group. The match proceeded smoothly, with each team scoring one goal in the first half. In the second half, Yuqing scored two goals, resulting in a 3-1 victory for Yuqing. After the defeat, the Jinan students were resentful and, in a fit of rage, attacked the Yuqing players and students with weapons, causing an unprecedented bloody tragedy in the sports world. It is reported that one of the leaders of the attack from Jinan is a well-known middle-distance runner in our country. The principal of Yuqing Middle School will file a lawsuit to resolve the matter through legal channels.

Details of the Attack: After the match, the Jinan cheering squad, like wolves and tigers, attacked and beat the Yuqing players and students. They used fists and feet, iron bars, and wooden clubs, and some even threatened with handguns. Seeing the situation was not good, Yuqing fled into the Xie Jin Hui writing room, and the Xie Jin Hui staff closed the door, thinking they were protecting them. However, the Jinan students, still enraged, swarmed forward and smashed all the glass windows of the writing room, breaking down the door and entering. The Yuqing students were like turtles in a jar, at the mercy of the attackers' beating. The writing room was also smashed to pieces, with blood all over the floor. Six people from Yuqing were seriously injured, and countless others were slightly injured.

Detained in the Sixth District: The Shen Yuan soccer field is located in the Chinese territory, under the jurisdiction of the Caojiadu Sixth District. Seeing the situation was not good, the Sports Association reported to the police station, which immediately dispatched police officers to the scene to suppress the violence and arrest several students. Later, officials from both schools sent people to the police station to request the release of the students. The police station released the detained students. The principal of Yuqing School immediately sent the injured to the hospital and plans to file a lawsuit against Jinan.

Injury Statistics: Six students from Yuqing Middle School were seriously injured: Liang Tiemin, 20 years old, from Guangdong, internal injuries; Wu Shoufu, 19 years old, from Fujian, head injury; Shen Qiusheng, 18 years old, local, left leg injury; Zheng Fei, 24 years old, local, left eye injury; Wu Jiugao, 23 years old, local, waist injury; Zhang Guanjin, 20 years old, local, head injury. They were sent to Baolong Hospital for treatment by the school principal.

Today's Matches Suspended: Today's middle school soccer match between Hujiang Affiliated High School and Pudong Middle School was originally scheduled to be held at Shen Yuan. However, because the Shen Yuan stadium is closed, the match will not be held today.

Tonight's Western YMCA Basketball

Western YMCA vs. Mailing Finals

Starting at 8:15 PM

Winner Takes the Championship
